<ul class="NavContent" style="list-style: none none; margin-left: 0; text-align: center; font-size: 105%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; line-height: inherit;"><li style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0"><div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_f8ff74de6c54a1c61ba742d0729d47bd"></map><img usemap="#timeline_f8ff74de6c54a1c61ba742d0729d47bd" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/f8ff74de6c54a1c61ba742d0729d47bd.png" /></div></li></ul>
</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2003 Brazilian Grand Prix</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> motor race held on 6 April 2003 at <a href="/wiki/Aut%C3%B3dromo_Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Pace" title="Autódromo José Carlos Pace">Autódromo José Carlos Pace</a> (Interlagos). It was attended by 120,000 spectators. It was the third round of the <a href="/wiki/2003_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2003 Formula One World Championship">2003 Formula One World Championship</a>, the 32nd <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="Brazilian Grand Prix">Brazilian Grand Prix</a> and the 700th Formula One World Championship race.
</p><p>The race was scheduled to run for 71 laps, but was stopped on lap 56 after two major crashes blocked the circuit. Due to confusion about the timing of the <a href="/wiki/Red_flag_(racing)" class="mw-redirect" title="Red flag (racing)">red flag</a>, the win was initially awarded to <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> of <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Giancarlo_Fisichella" title="Giancarlo Fisichella">Giancarlo Fisichella</a> of <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">Jordan</a> in second and <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> of <a href="/wiki/Renault" title="Renault">Renault</a> in third. However, following a post-race appeal by the Jordan team, eventually heard in court, it was established that Fisichella was leading when the race results were declared, and he was awarded the win with Räikkönen demoted to second. Alonso remained in third place; he had missed the podium ceremony at the time as he was receiving medical attention. The race, which was Jordan's 4th and final victory, was the team's 200th Grand Prix.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> This was the first victory for a <a href="/wiki/Ford_Motor_Company" title="Ford Motor Company">Ford</a> engine since the <a href="/wiki/1999_European_Grand_Prix" title="1999 European Grand Prix">1999 European Grand Prix</a>, and the first victory for an Italian driver since <a href="/wiki/Riccardo_Patrese" title="Riccardo Patrese">Riccardo Patrese</a> won the <a href="/wiki/1992_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1992 Japanese Grand Prix">1992 Japanese Grand Prix</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg/220px-Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg/330px-Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/eb/Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg 2x" data-file-width="349" data-file-height="197" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Interlagos_2006_aerial.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Aut%C3%B3dromo_Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Pace" title="Autódromo José Carlos Pace">Autódromo José Carlos Pace</a> <i>(pictured in 2006)</i>, where the race was held.</div></div></div>
<p>The 2003 <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="Brazilian Grand Prix">Brazilian Grand Prix</a> was the third of sixteen scheduled <a href="/wiki/Open-wheel_racing" class="mw-redirect" title="Open-wheel racing">single seater</a> motor races of the <a href="/wiki/2003_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2003 Formula One World Championship">2003 Formula One World Championship</a>, the 32nd edition of the event and the 700th Formula One World Championship round. It took place at the 15-turn 4.309&#160;km (2.677&#160;mi) <a href="/wiki/Aut%C3%B3dromo_Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Pace" title="Autódromo José Carlos Pace">Autódromo José Carlos Pace</a> in the Brazilian city of <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo</a> on 6 April 2003.<sup id="cite_ref-CF1Race_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CF1Race-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> The bumpy track placed a large amount of strain and <a href="/wiki/G-force" title="G-force">g-force</a> onto a driver.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> To compensate for <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_car" title="Formula One car">cars</a> being driven over its bumpy surface, teams employed a computer programme fed into a chassis to reconstruct every movement under undulation.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Under a <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA; Formula One's governing body) regulation mandating Formula One's two <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_tyres" title="Formula One tyres">tyre</a> suppliers <a href="/wiki/Bridgestone" title="Bridgestone">Bridgestone</a> and <a href="/wiki/Michelin" title="Michelin">Michelin</a> to bring a single wet-weather tyre compound to each race to lower operating costs:<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-7">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Michelin brought the full wets and Bridgestone the intermediates.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianRace_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianRace-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After winning the <a href="/wiki/2003_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2003 Malaysian Grand Prix">Malaysian Grand Prix</a> two weeks earlier, <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a> with 16 <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>, six ahead of his teammate <a href="/wiki/David_Coulthard" title="David Coulthard">David Coulthard</a> in second. <a href="/wiki/Juan_Pablo_Montoya" title="Juan Pablo Montoya">Juan Pablo Montoya</a> of <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Rubens_Barrichello" title="Rubens Barrichello">Rubens Barrichello</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> for <a href="/wiki/Renault_in_Formula_One" title="Renault in Formula One">Renault</a> tied for third with eight points each.<sup id="cite_ref-2003Points_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2003Points-9">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">World Constructors' Championship</a>, McLaren led with 26 points; Ferrari and Renault were tied for second position with 16 points. Williams were a further two points behind in fourth and <a href="/wiki/Sauber_Motorsport" title="Sauber Motorsport">Sauber</a> rounded out the top five with four points.<sup id="cite_ref-2003Points_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2003Points-9">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Following the <a href="/wiki/2002_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Brazilian Grand Prix">2002 edition</a>, race organisers invested $1.7 million in resurfacing 1&#160;km (0.62&#160;mi) of track surface in an attempt to reduce its bumpiness, rebuilt its drainage system and introduced <a href="/wiki/Run-off_area" title="Run-off area">run-off areas</a> in the first seven turns.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In preparation for the race, the majority of teams conducted in-season test sessions at the <a href="/wiki/Circuit_de_Barcelona-Catalunya" title="Circuit de Barcelona-Catalunya">Circuit de Catalunya</a> (now called the Circuit de Barcelona-Catalunya) in Spain from 25 to 28 March 2003 and worked to alter the aerodynamic performance of their cars. Sauber and Williams evaluated revised chassis components and both teams assessed their selection of tyre compounds from the Malaysian Grand Prix, optimising the <a href="/wiki/Racing_setup" title="Racing setup">setup</a> of their vehicles to better suit it.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Test_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Test-11">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> A lap of 1 minute and 17.288 seconds topped the time sheets for the Williams <a href="/wiki/Test_driver" title="Test driver">test driver</a> <a href="/wiki/Marc_Gen%C3%A9" title="Marc Gené">Marc Gené</a> on the first day.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pedro_de_la_Rosa" title="Pedro de la Rosa">Pedro de la Rosa</a>, the McLaren test driver, set the second day's fastest time, a 1 minute and 15.506 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Test_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Test-11">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Williams' <a href="/wiki/Ralf_Schumacher" title="Ralf Schumacher">Ralf Schumacher</a> set the quickest lap on the third day, lowering the overall best time to a 1 minute and 15.352 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> On the final day (held in heavy rain in the morning and sunshine for most of the afternoon) Ralf Schumacher remained fastest overall with a lap of 1 minute and 17.591 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportTest4_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportTest4-14">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Racing_(Formula_One_team)" title="Toyota Racing (Formula One team)">Toyota</a> test driver <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Zonta" title="Ricardo Zonta">Ricardo Zonta</a> drove a <a href="/wiki/Toyota_TF102" title="Toyota TF102">Toyota TF102B</a> for three days at the <a href="/wiki/Circuit_Paul_Ricard" title="Circuit Paul Ricard">Circuit Paul Ricard</a> evaluating its tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportTest4_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportTest4-14">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The defending World Drivers' Champion <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> of Ferrari was criticised by the German and Italian press for a sub-par beginning to the season. Schumacher said he expected criticism and thought Ferrari would have an advantage on circuits that suited his team better than others,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> "The first two races are not too good. Still, we got eight points out of these not very good races for us and our time will come again."<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen, the Drivers Championship leader, said he would approach the race in the same method as he did in the preceding Malaysian Grand Prix,<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> as <a href="/wiki/Giancarlo_Fisichella" title="Giancarlo Fisichella">Giancarlo Fisichella</a> was eager to score for the <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">Jordan</a> team in its 200th Formula One race, "I trained and prepared hard for Sepang but unfortunately I did not get off the mark. So my target for the Brazilian Grand Prix is to take the chequered flag and bring points to the team and looking at the way the car ran strongly with Ralph in Malaysia, I know I can get both jobs done."<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg/220px-Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg/330px-Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg/440px-Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Justin_Wilson_2007.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Justin_Wilson_(racing_driver)" title="Justin Wilson (racing driver)">Justin Wilson</a> <i>(pictured in 2007)</i> was deemed fit to compete in Brazil after his arms were temporarily paralysed by a loose <a href="/wiki/HANS_device" title="HANS device">HANS device</a> at the preceding <a href="/wiki/2003_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2003 Malaysian Grand Prix">Malaysian Grand Prix</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Two weeks before the Grand Prix, the FIA announced drivers would no longer be granted dispensation to compete in Formula One races without wearing a <a href="/wiki/HANS_device" title="HANS device">HANS device</a>. It stated any competitor who could not wear a HANS device for medical reasons would be barred from driving in future events.<sup id="cite_ref-IndyMar03_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IndyMar03-19">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> This stance was ratified at a meeting of the <a href="/wiki/FIA_World_Motor_Sport_Council" title="FIA World Motor Sport Council">FIA World Motor Sport Council</a> in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> on 2 April.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Minardi" title="Minardi">Minardi</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Justin_Wilson_(racing_driver)" title="Justin Wilson (racing driver)">Justin Wilson</a> was passed fit by the FIA medical delegate <a href="/wiki/Sid_Watkins" title="Sid Watkins">Sid Watkins</a> to take part in the event.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> At the previous race, Wilson suffered from pain in his shoulders which was caused by a loose HANS device and <a href="/wiki/Seat_belt" title="Seat belt">seat belt</a>, causing him to move about freely in his car's <a href="/wiki/Cockpit" title="Cockpit">cockpit</a> and pinching a nerve that paralysed both his arms. Wilson visited the team's headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Faenza" title="Faenza">Faenza</a>, Italy to test a twin seat belt system installed in his car to prevent a similar occurrence.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello, who had a minor <a href="/wiki/Hernia" title="Hernia">hernia</a> and received dispensation from the stewards not to wear a HANS device for medical reasons,<sup id="cite_ref-IndyMar03_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IndyMar03-19">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> was at risk of being dropped for the race in the event a solution to his discomfort was not found.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He tested a new HANS device during free practice and reported no discomfort,<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> leaving the services of the Ferrari reserve driver <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> unneeded.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;note 2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BarrichelloGP_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BarrichelloGP-25">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Some teams made changes to their vehicles for the event.<sup id="cite_ref-Piola_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Piola-27">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Williams installed a revised <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a> unit and rear <a href="/wiki/Car_suspension" title="Car suspension">suspension</a> bracket designed specially for the <a href="/wiki/Williams_FW25" title="Williams FW25">FW25</a>. The team also fitted a revised specification of front wing, modified a terminal section of the car's bodywork and rectified a <a href="/wiki/Spoiler_(car)" title="Spoiler (car)">rear wing</a> issue. The Ferrari and Renault teams introduced new specifications of rear wing: Ferrari's wing changes featured semi-circular holes in the outer part of its main profile to limit vortex and was used solely by Barrichello. Renault adopted a rear wing characterised by a sinuous shape of its profiles, which was stood up sharply in the bulkheads section.<sup id="cite_ref-Piola_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Piola-27">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Private_test_session">Private test session</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Private test session">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>On Friday morning, a two-hour test session took place for teams who opted for limited testing during the season.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> In variable weather conditions that saw rain fell 90 minutes in,<sup id="cite_ref-F1TestBrazil_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1TestBrazil-29">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Renault driver <a href="/wiki/Jarno_Trulli" title="Jarno Trulli">Jarno Trulli</a> set the session's fastest lap, a 1 minute and 14.262 seconds. <a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B4nio_Pizzonia" title="Antônio Pizzonia">Antônio Pizzonia</a> was second in a Jaguar and his teammate <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> third. Alonso, Fisichella, <a href="/wiki/Allan_McNish" title="Allan McNish">Allan McNish</a>, the Renault test driver, Minardi's <a href="/wiki/Jos_Verstappen" title="Jos Verstappen">Jos Verstappen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Firman" title="Ralph Firman">Ralph Firman</a> for Jordan and Wilson made up positions four to nine.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1BrazilTest_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1BrazilTest-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> During the session, Pizzonia drove the spare Jaguar after a mechanical fault stopped his race car at the Subida dos Boxes corner.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1BrazilTest_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1BrazilTest-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportBrazilTest_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportBrazilTest-31">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> With 36 minutes remaining, Firman abandoned his car in the pit lane with a <a href="/wiki/Drive_shaft" title="Drive shaft">drive shaft</a> problem.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1BrazilTest_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1BrazilTest-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Alonso subsequently spun on the Reta Oposta <a href="/wiki/Straight_(racing)" title="Straight (racing)">straight</a> and was beached in a <a href="/wiki/Run-off_area" title="Run-off area">gravel trap</a> at the Descida do Lago turn.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportBrazilTest_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportBrazilTest-31">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> His Renault was undamaged.<sup id="cite_ref-F1TestBrazil_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1TestBrazil-29">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id="Practice.2C_qualifying_and_warm-up_sessions"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Practice,_qualifying_and_warm-up_sessions">Practice, qualifying and warm-up sessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Practice, qualifying and warm-up sessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Three practice sessions were held before the Sunday race: one 60-minute session on Friday morning and two 45-minute sessions on Saturday morning.<sup id="cite_ref-2003Regs_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2003Regs-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> In the first practice session, held in torrential weather conditions and saw four drivers record no lap times,<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher was quickest with a lap of 1 minute and 28.060 seconds, followed by Coulthard, <a href="/wiki/British_American_Racing" title="British American Racing">British American Racing</a> (BAR) driver <a href="/wiki/Jenson_Button" title="Jenson Button">Jenson Button</a>, Trulli, Montoya, Barrichello, the Toyota pair of <a href="/wiki/Olivier_Panis" title="Olivier Panis">Olivier Panis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_da_Matta" title="Cristiano da Matta">Cristiano da Matta</a>, Fisichella and <a href="/wiki/Heinz-Harald_Frentzen" title="Heinz-Harald Frentzen">Heinz-Harald Frentzen</a> of Sauber.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Seconds after Räikkönen exited the pit lane, he lost control of his vehicle into the Reta Oposta straight and spun onto some grass.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-35">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> He narrowly avoided a collision with a barrier to his left.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-35">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> With fifteen minutes to go,<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_33-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Pizzonia crashed heavily leaving the Curva do Sol turn and struck the barriers on both sides of the circuit on his first timed lap,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-35">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> temporarily stopping the session so that his Jaguar car could be removed from the track.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_33-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> After the session restarted, Alonso slid on the wet track and made minor contact against a wall at the Senna S chicane.<sup id="cite_ref-AF1FP1_33-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AF1FP1-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The torrential rain observed in the first session prompted several drivers to express concerns they would lose control of their vehicles and crash in those conditions.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Around twenty minutes before the first qualifying session began,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportPetition_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportPetition-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard, a senior member of the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_Drivers%27_Association" title="Grand Prix Drivers&#39; Association">Grand Prix Drivers' Association</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-7">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Trulli and Michael Schumacher wrote a petition mandating the FIA cancel the session if there was no improvement in the track conditions.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportPetition_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportPetition-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> The petition was signed by a majority of drivers;<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> it was later disregarded after it was unable to be sent to everyone in time and race officials had deemed the circuit safe to drive on after the rain tapered off before qualifying commenced.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Villeneuve" title="Jacques Villeneuve">Jacques Villeneuve</a> of BAR said the petition was detrimental to Formula One, "What would it bring to Formula One for us not to go and qualify? People would think that we are just a bunch of sissies. We can't do that. We are paid a whole lot of money and it would be an insult to the fans."<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mark_Webber_2005.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Mark_Webber_2005.jpg/220px-Mark_Webber_2005.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Mark_Webber_2005.jpg/330px-Mark_Webber_2005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Mark_Webber_2005.jpg/440px-Mark_Webber_2005.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mark_Webber_2005.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> <i>(pictured in 2005 while driving for Williams)</i> took provisional <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> in the first qualifying session</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#Q" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">Qualifying</a> was split into two one-hour sessions; the first was held on Friday afternoon, and the second on Saturday afternoon. The first session's starting order was determined by the World Drivers' Championship order (first to last) and the second was run in reverse of the first session times (slowest to fastest). Each competitor was limited to one lap per session and the starting order was determined by the second session's fastest times.<sup id="cite_ref-2003Regs_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2003Regs-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The level of standing water fluctuated during the session. Webber took provisional <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> on a drying track with a 1 minute and 23.249 seconds lap. He was 0.138 seconds faster than Barrichello in second, who had pole until Webber's lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQ1_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQ1-43">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen, the first driver to set a lap, finished the session third and his teammate Coulthard was fourth after a driver error at Bico de Pato corner. Michael Schumacher <a href="/wiki/Aquaplaning" title="Aquaplaning">aquaplaned</a> shortly after he exited the pit lane and took fifth. Panis' Toyota was not setup for the wet-weather conditions and took sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Villeneuve was seventh;<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Pizzonia drove the spare Jaguar and took eighth notwithstanding him aquaplaning on the start/finish straight.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alonso elected to be circumspect en route to ninth,<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> as Frentzen in tenth reported an adequate car balance.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> An incorrect setup put Da Matta 11th.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> The wet-weather conditions restricted Trulli to 12th and an unbalanced car in corners taken at a slow speed left Ralf Schumacher in 13th. An <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">oversteer</a> and lack of grip restricted Fisichella to 14th as Verstappen extracted additional performance from his car to finish in 15th.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Heidfeld was circumspect through the Arquibancdas turn en route to 16th.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Montoya in 17th lost control of the rear of his Williams under braking and went onto a concrete run-off area at Ferradura corner.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQ1_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQ1-43">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Firman in 18th drove with the rear of Jordan's spare car attached to his race vehicle.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Wilson avoided a spin on the start/finish straight and was 19th.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Button was the only driver not to set a lap time: he had a sudden oversteer when he ran onto a damp white line denoting the track boundaries,<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ScotsmanQ1_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ScotsmanQ1-46">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> and aquaplaned at almost 145&#160;mph (233&#160;km/h).<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Button went through two polystyrene boards, removed his car's rear wing and abandoned the attempt.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ1_44-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ1-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ1_45-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ1-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> The session was temporarily stopped to clear on-track debris.<sup id="cite_ref-DTQuali_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTQuali-7">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ScotsmanQ1_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ScotsmanQ1-46">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Barrichello_2002.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Barrichello_2002.jpg/170px-Barrichello_2002.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="298" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Barrichello_2002.jpg/255px-Barrichello_2002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Barrichello_2002.jpg/340px-Barrichello_2002.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1128" data-file-height="1975" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Barrichello_2002.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Rubens_Barrichello" title="Rubens Barrichello">Rubens Barrichello</a> <i>(pictured in 2002)</i> took the seventh <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> of his career in the second qualifying session</div></div></div>
<p>The circuit was sodden for the beginning of the second practice session and dried as it progressed to provide every driver with dry track acclimatisation.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello set the pace with a 1 minute and 14.071 seconds lap. Ralf Schumacher, Montoya, Michael Schumacher, Alonso, Räikkönen, Pizzonia, Webber, Coulthard and Heidfeld made up positions two to ten.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> In warm weather conditions, the final practice session was led by Panis who recorded a time of 1 minute and 13.457 seconds, ahead of Michael Schumacher, Trulli, Coulthard, Montoya, Räikkönen, Barrichello, Webber, Ralf Schumacher and Alonso. Several competitors spun during the session; none sustained damage to their cars.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen paced a fifteen-minute warm-up session that took place before the second qualifying session with a lap of 1 minute and 13.886 seconds. Barrichello, Michael Schumacher, Coulthard, Montoya, Webber, Button, Ralf Schumacher, Villeneuve and Heidfeld were second to tenth.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The second qualifying session was held in warm and dry weather conditions.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ2_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ2-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello had the lap time display on his <a href="/wiki/Steering_wheel" title="Steering wheel">steering wheel</a> switched off so he could be focused.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> This earned him pole position, the first for a Brazilian driver at the track since <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">Ayrton Senna</a> in the <a href="/wiki/1994_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Brazilian Grand Prix">1994 event</a>, his first since the <a href="/wiki/2002_Hungarian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Hungarian Grand Prix">2002 Hungarian Grand Prix</a> and the seventh of his career with a 1 minute and 13.807 seconds lap.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello was joined on the grid's front row by Coulthard who was 0.11 seconds slower after McLaren changed his car's balance.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Webber was set to take pole position until a driver error at Pinheirinho demoted him to third.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-STimesQ2_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STimesQ2-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> A driver error at the same turn and a loose car left Räikkönen in fourth as Trulli moved to fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Excessive oversteer and circumspect braking restricted Ralf Schumacher to sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ2_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ2-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher made a minor error at the Senna S chicane and was seventh;<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> he took his lowest grid position since he started ninth at the <a href="/wiki/1998_German_Grand_Prix" title="1998 German Grand Prix">1998 German Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-STimesQ2_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STimesQ2-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Fisichella qualified eighth, Montoya had an oversteer that put him ninth and Alonso was tenth.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Button set the 11th-fastest lap, with his teammate Villeneuve 13th after an intermittent loss of power in the Senna S chicane; Heidfeld in 12th separated the pair. Frentzen took 14th and Panis (who made a driver error) 15th.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ2_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ2-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Firman changed his car's setup and qualified 16th due to a driver error,<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ2_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ2-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> ahead of Pizzonia in 17th, who had brake problems and an unbalanced car.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> An tight handling car and an unsuccessful fix to the problems left Da Matta in 18th. The Minardi cars were equipped with a hard compound tyre and completed the starting order in 19th and 20th (Verstappen ahead of Wilson).<sup id="cite_ref-FIAQ2_52-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAQ2-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMQ2_53-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMQ2-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>

<th colspan="10"><div class="center" style="width:auto; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;">Source:<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Race">Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>On the morning of 6 April, McLaren sought permission from the FIA to change Räikkönen's engine after a crack in its casting was detected via <a href="/wiki/Telemetry" title="Telemetry">telemetry</a>. The FIA authorised the engine switch after it analysed data proving the engine was damaged. Telemetry from BAR also detected damage to Villeneuve's engine and were also allowed to change it.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Rain was forecast for the race; at the start the track was flooded because of a torrential downpour that fell from at 11:00 <a href="/wiki/Time_in_Brazil" title="Time in Brazil">Brasilia Time</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%E2%88%9202:00" title="UTC−02:00">UTC−02:00</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> 120,000 spectators attended the Grand Prix.<sup id="cite_ref-TimesFerrariDNF_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TimesFerrariDNF-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> It was due to commence at 14:00 local time,<sup id="cite_ref-CF1Race_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CF1Race-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> before the FIA race director <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Whiting" title="Charlie Whiting">Charlie Whiting</a> delayed it for fifteen minutes,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> to enable standing water to be drained from the circuit.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Event organisers permitted teams to alter the setup of their cars to run on a sodden track, specially the wings and <a href="/wiki/Ride_height" title="Ride height">ride heights</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> The standing water caused heavy spray and impaired visibility, and all vehicles used wet-weather tyre compounds.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> The track's deficient drainage caused a large amount of water to cascade from a slope onto the tarmac surface at the Curva do Sol corner and made it susceptible for cars to aquaplane.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianRace_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianRace-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ITVRace_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ITVRace-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The race began behind the safety car,<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> with no <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#F" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">formation lap</a>; notwithstanding the slow speed drivers struggled for grip on the flooded track surface.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Some drivers (including Verstappen, Frentzen, Pizzonia, Panis, Fisichella and Firman) elected to make pit stops for fuel under safety car conditions in an attempt to avoid having to make a second pit stop later in the race.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> After the rain had stopped,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> the safety car drove into the pit lane at the end of lap eight, and cars were allowed to overtake.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello bunched up the field on the approach to the start/finish line;<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> the manoeuvre failed to work and Coulthard passed him for the lead under braking for the Senna S chicane.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello was circumspect for the rest of the lap as Webber and Räikkönen pressured him.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Further down the order, Montoya moved from ninth to fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Heidfeld became the Grand Prix's first retirement on lap nine when his engineers informed him over the radio of an oil feed problem that cut out his engine. He pulled off to the side of the track to ensure that no oil was deposited on the <a href="/wiki/Racing_line" title="Racing line">racing line</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg/170px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg/255px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg/340px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimi_Raikkonen_2002_Taiwan.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> <i>(pictured in 2002)</i> was initially declared the winner of the race due to a timekeeping error.</div></div></div>
<p>On lap ten, Räikkönen overtook Barrichello for second at the Senna S chicane and lost third when Montoya passed him later that lap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> There were overtakes further down the field on that lap. Ralf Schumacher moved past Trulli for sixth and Pizzonia passed Verstappen for fifteenth.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On the 11th lap, Räikkönen closed up to his teammate Coulthard and passed him to take the lead on the approach to the Senna S chicane. Not long after Montoya overtook Coulthard for third at the end of the Reta Oposta straight that leads to the Descida do Lago corner. That same lap, Ralf Schumacher and Trulli made contact, causing the former to spin.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Webber then overtook Barrichello for fourth and Michael Schumacher did the same on his teammate soon after for fifth. Ralf Schumacher began to recover lost positions with an overtake on Villeneuve for tenth on the 12th lap. At the front of the field, Räikkönen had increased his lead over Montoya to five seconds by lap 14.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On the same lap,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Montoya reported a loss of rear tyre grip to his team over the radio and ran wide leaving Juncao turn. Coulthard overtook Montoya for second.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the circuit began to dry,<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> except for turn three which continued to have water stream across it,<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard began to close up to his teammate Räikkönen,<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> as Michael Schumacher overtook Webber on the inside for fourth on lap 15 leaving Arquibancdas turn.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On the 16th lap,<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Michael Schumacher moved into third position with a pass on the slower Montoya around the outside at the Bico de Pato corner.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Wilson drove through a river at the Curva do Sol turn and aquaplaned off another on the following lap. He retired after he was unable to restart his car.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard drew close enough to his teammate Räikkönen by the 18th lap, just as Barrichello moved past Webber for fifth place.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> That same lap, Firman's right-front suspension system failed on the start/finish straight,<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> causing him to lose control of his car and his flailing right-front wheel narrowly avoided striking its cockpit.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianRace_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianRace-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He narrowly avoided a collision with his teammate Fisichella,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCFisiWin_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCFisiWin-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> struck the rear of Panis' car at almost 190&#160;mph (310&#160;km/h).<sup id="cite_ref-TimesRace_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TimesRace-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Panis' rear wing was removed and the front of Firman's car sustained damage.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>The safety car was deployed for the second time for debris clearing.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Several drivers took the opportunity to make pit stops for fuel and tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Montoya avoided a collision with Trulli and Alonso stopped twice since he had the incorrect tyres installed on his car.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> The safety car was withdrawn at the end of lap 22 and Räikkönen closed the field up to maintain the lead from Coulthard, Michael Schumacher and the yet-to-stop Da Matta.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> On the Reta Oposta straight, Barrichello overtook Da Matta for fourth on lap 23,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> as a driver error dropped Frentzen from eighth to sixteenth and Ralf Schumacher passed Verstappen for eleventh. Montoya overtook Da Matta for fifth and Ralf Schumacher moved past Button for ninth during lap 24.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On the 25th lap, Montoya aquaplaned at the Curva do Sol and crashed into a right-hand side barrier.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Pizzonia hit the water stream flowing across the circuit at the same corner and aquaplaned.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> He collided with the wall, ricocheted off it and struck Montoya's car. The accidents elevated Da Matta to fifth and Webber to sixth. By lap 26, Alonso had passed Villeneuve and Fisichella to move to tenth.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Michael_Schumacher_01_(sk).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg/170px-Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="185" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg/255px-Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg/340px-Michael_Schumacher_01_%28sk%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="991" data-file-height="1077" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Michael_Schumacher_01_(sk).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> <i>(pictured in 2007)</i> was one of six drivers to be caught out by a stream of water at the Curva do Sol corner</div></div></div>
<p>Lap 27 saw the third safety car deployment: Michael Schumacher aquaplaned off the stream of water at the Curva do Sol turn and avoided hitting a recovery crane extricating Montoya and Pizzonia's vehicles from the side of the track.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> He stopped on a run-off area and failed to finish a race for the first time since the <a href="/wiki/2001_German_Grand_Prix" title="2001 German Grand Prix">2001 German Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen and Da Matta made their pit stops for fuel under safety car conditions. Coulthard took the lead and maintained it at the lap 30 <a href="/wiki/Rolling_start" title="Rolling start">restart</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen overtook Fisichella and Verstappen to return to seventh position and Da Matta passed Frentzen.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On the 31st lap, Verstappen aquaplaned on the stream of water at the Curva do Sol corner and retired.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> The water caught out Button on lap 33:<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> he lost control of his vehicle and crashed heavily against the barrier. Button was unhurt.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> The accident necessitated the safety car's fourth deployment.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> In the meantime, his teammate Villeneuve spun and fell behind Frentzen and Trulli. During the safety car period, Da Matta made a pit stop to correct a technical problem. At the lap 37 restart, Da Matta and Webber passed Villeneuve.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Räikkönen overtook Alonso on the start/finish straight into the Senna S chicane for fourth on the 38th lap.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Further round the lap, he passed Ralf Schumacher on the outside line going into the Descida do Lago corner.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen in eighth was overtaken by Webber and Villeneuve re-passed Da Matta for tenth during the same lap.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On lap 40, Alonso steered to the inside to extract additional grip and passed Ralf Schumacher at Mergulho turn for fourth position.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> As Barrichello gained on race leader Coulthard, the stewards informed Renault on the 42nd lap that Alonso had been issued a drive-through penalty because he was deemed to have overtaken Ralf Schumacher under yellow flag conditions.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> He took the penalty on the same lap and fell from fourth to ninth.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On the 44th lap, Webber lost control of the rear of his car at the Curva do Sol corner and spun through 360 degrees. He avoided contact with the barrier and merged onto the track after Frentzen, Alonso and Villeneuve passed him.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>
At the front of the field, Coulthard (on worn tyres) ran wide on the approach to the Senna S chicane and Barrichello used the driver error to pass him for first position on lap 45.<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello began to pull away from Coulthard, extending his lead to 4.2 seconds by lap 46's conclusion, who in turn, was 15 seconds ahead of his teammate Räikkönen.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On lap 47,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello pulled off at the side of the circuit to retire from the Brazilian Grand Prix for the ninth consecutive time.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> A fuel feed problem was suspected to have caused Barrichello's retirement until it was traced to a malfunctioning in-car computer calculating it had 12&#160;l (2.6&#160;imp&#160;gal; 3.2&#160;US&#160;gal) more fuel than normal and an error with Ferrari's telemetry did not inform the team he had run out of fuel.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard returned to the lead, eighteen seconds ahead of his teammate Räikkönen in second and Fisichella third.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> By the 48th lap, drivers became concerned over fuel. Ralf Schumacher made a pit stop and rejoined in ninth. Alonso and Frentzen overtook Trulli and demoted him to sixth during laps 49 and 50.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> </p><div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg/170px-Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg/255px-Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg/340px-Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1752" data-file-height="2628" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Alonso_usgp_2004_pits.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> <i>(pictured in 2004)</i> sustained a major accident that contributed to an premature conclusion to the Grand Prix.</div></div></div><p>On the 52nd lap,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Coulthard made a pit stop for tyres after a minor loss of car control through Juncao corner and the start/finish straight.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> He rejoined the race in fourth position.<sup id="cite_ref-ITVRace_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ITVRace-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen retook the lead with the faster Fisichella second and Alonso third. On lap 54, a lack of tyre grip caused Räikkönen to understeer on the approach to the Mergulho turn and Fisichella passed him to claim the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Both drivers were borderline on fuel and it appeared Coulthard would return to the lead and win the event.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> At Arquibancadas corner, Webber attempted to prevent his tyres from overheating wherever possible and lost car grip on lap 54.<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> He lost control of his car, and crashed heavily against the concrete barriers on each side of the circuit before the start/finish straight at 240&#160;km/h (150&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WebberHS_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberHS-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Debris from Webber's car and three of its tyres were strewn across the track and causing the safety car's fifth deployment.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_61-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Webber clambered from his car unhurt.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Fisichella and Räikkönen negotiated their way through the debris and the latter entered the pit lane to stop for fuel.<sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Alonso did not notice the waved yellow flags informing him of a hazard,<sup id="cite_ref-ITVRace_64-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ITVRace-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> because he was discussing whether to use dry or wet tyres with Renault over the radio.<sup id="cite_ref-AlonsoCrash_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlonsoCrash-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> He hit one of Webber's detached rear wheels at around 270&#160;km/h (170&#160;mph) in an impact measured at 4.5&#160;<i>g<sub>0</sub></i> (44&#160;m/s<sup>2</sup>).<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AlonsoCrash_74-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlonsoCrash-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Alonso veered left and struck a tyre wall at 35&#160;<i>g<sub>0</sub></i> (340&#160;m/s<sup>2</sup>) lateral and longitudinal. He was launched broadside across the circuit and into a concrete barrier at 60&#160;<i>g<sub>0</sub></i> (590&#160;m/s<sup>2</sup>).<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AlonsoCrash_74-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlonsoCrash-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Alonso sustained a bruised left elbow, knee and thigh,<sup id="cite_ref-CrashNetAlonso_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashNetAlonso-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> a group of medical personnel placed him on a stretcher for transport by ambulance to the Saint Louis Hospital in São Paulo for observation.<sup id="cite_ref-MCOMRace_66-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MCOMRace-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AlonsoRenault_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlonsoRenault-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Because of a large amount of debris, personnel tending to Alonso, and 75 per cent of the race completed, its continuation behind the safety car was impossible. The race ended early with a <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_regulations#Flags" title="Formula One regulations">red flag</a> and all cars returned to the pit lane.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Fisichella's car overheated because the safety car was slow and fire emerged from the engine bay as he stopped in <i><a href="/wiki/Parc_ferm%C3%A9" title="Parc fermé">parc fermé</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-F1NetRace_62-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1NetRace-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIARace_65-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIARace-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCFisiWin_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCFisiWin-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> Under <i>Article 154 of the 2003 Formula One Sporting Regulations</i>, the race was "deemed to have finished when the leading car crossed the line at the end of the lap two laps prior to that lap during which the signal to stop was given" in the event more than 75 percent of it was completed.<sup id="cite_ref-2003Regs_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2003Regs-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The official timekeeping screens first showed that Fisichella had begun his 56th lap; then this status briefly disappeared and displayed it as on his 55th. The race stewards based their decision on the belief Fisichella was still on his 55th lap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCRuling_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCRuling-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Fisichella celebrated with the Jordan team in the belief he had won before they were informed Räikkönen had won;<sup id="cite_ref-:0_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> the latter was told of the decision as he was weighed.<sup id="cite_ref-TimesRace_70-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TimesRace-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Alonso was third, Coulthard fourth, the non-stopping Frentzen fifth, Villeneuve sixth, Webber seventh (notwithstanding his crash) and Trulli eighth.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashRace_67-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashRace-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Ralf Schumacher and Da Matta (who had oversteer) were the final provisional finishers.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-race">Post-race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Post-race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Because Alonso was in hospital, Räikkönen and Fisichella appeared on the podium to collect their trophies and spoke to the media in a later press conference.<sup id="cite_ref-ITVRace_64-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ITVRace-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen stated his belief he was lucky to be awarded the victory: "I think that it came so quickly that we didn't make the decision quickly enough but in the end it was the right decision, so thanks to the team. It was a difficult race because the conditions were so bad and the safety car was out so often, but I'm pretty happy."<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Fisichella said he was disappointed about the race's situation: "first of all for Fernando, I hope that he's alright and then also because I won the race but the rules say that when there is a red flag, the result is taken from one lap before (two laps in fact) so I am very sorry about that but I never thought I would finish in second position so it's a great day anyway."<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alonso received messages of well-being from the public and rally driver <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Sainz" title="Carlos Sainz">Carlos Sainz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AlonsoRenault_76-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlonsoRenault-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> He was discharged from hospital after 12 hours,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCAlonsoCrash_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCAlonsoCrash-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> and returned to <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a> on the morning of 8 April to begin physical therapy for the season's next race, the <a href="/wiki/2003_San_Marino_Grand_Prix" title="2003 San Marino Grand Prix">San Marino Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashNetAlonso_75-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashNetAlonso-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Alonso commented on the accident: "I thought my race was going pretty well. But then I came round the final corner to find debris everywhere and I had nowhere to go. I think I hit a wheel, and the next thing I knew I was headed for the barriers."<sup id="cite_ref-BBCAlonsoCrash_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCAlonsoCrash-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> He attributed the HANS device for preventing him from sustaining more serious injuries.<sup id="cite_ref-AlonsoCrash_74-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlonsoCrash-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Webber was not required to take a medical test and performed 60 <a href="/wiki/Push-up" title="Push-up">push-ups</a> to persuade his physiotherapist he had suffered no long-term complications from his crash.<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> He called it "the biggest accident I've had in a Formula One car" and revealed his neck and knees took most of the force from the impact: "I haven't been in a race that crazy before and it's the most damage I've done to a Formula One car. I've knocked two corners off before but nothing like this."<sup id="cite_ref-WebberHS_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberHS-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The way in which Alonso and Michael Schumacher crashed put them at risk of sanctioning by the FIA. An FIA observer reported Schumacher and Alonso to the governing body; the stewards could not question Alonso in Brazil because he was hospitalised. Schumacher was interviewed by the race director Charlie Whiting at the San Marino Grand Prix pre-event drivers' meeting on 17 April.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, Alonso and Schumacher had separate meetings with Whiting; he cautioned the two over their future driving standards and did not further reprimand them.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Villeneuve said he felt the drivers and not the track conditions contributed to the unsafe racing observed in the Grand Prix: "It is down to the drivers to be less crazy in those conditions and there was some crazy driving out there. Some drivers were overtaking under the yellow flags, halfway through the race I saw Alonso overtake under the flags. I think that is the kind of driving that leads to big accidents."<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> After his first race retirement since the 2001 German Grand Prix, Michael Schumacher stated he was not worried about the possibility of him winning his sixth World Drivers' Championship: "In terms of the championship, obviously it would have been better for us if Fisichella had won the race in Brazil instead of Raikkonen, especially as Giancarlo drove a good race anyway. But the gap to the championship leader is not so big, given there are still 13 races, so there is no need to be concerned about it."<sup id="cite_ref-TimesFerrariDNF_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TimesFerrariDNF-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Barrichello said he would continue to strive for a win at the Brazilian Grand Prix and was frustrated to learn a fuel problem caused his retirement: "I feel an enormous disappointment but I am not losing hope. I will not stop racing until I win in this country."<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Coulthard said he was annoyed with himself for making a pit stop before the red flags were shown because he believed he could have won the race had he not done so: "I am going away from here without a grand prix win that I worked hard for. I believe I have more claim on that victory than other people. I'd done my final stop of the race and I know the three guys in front of me all had to come in again if the race had not been stopped."<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Frentzen lauded Sauber's decision to change its strategy that saw him start the event in the team's spare car: "At the end of the day it turned out to be the right decision. It was not easy to run with a full tank and I had a lot of aquaplaning which made me spin once. But we finished fifth and scored four points, so I am very happy about this result."<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Paul_Stoddart" title="Paul Stoddart">Paul Stoddart</a>, the Minardi team owner, claimed they could have taken victory had both its cars been running: "Today saw possibly the first time ever that Minardi was potentially in a genuine, race-winning position. Many people may laugh, but only those of us within the team will ever know the truth. We had the strategy, but not the luck."<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRaceNotes_68-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRaceNotes-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Timekeeping_error">Timekeeping error</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Timekeeping error">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After he flew to London from Brazil on the morning of 8 April, Whiting launched an internal investigation into the result of the race because FIA officials were unhappy at the timesheets provided to the governing body by Formula One's timekeepers <a href="/wiki/TAG_Heuer" title="TAG Heuer">TAG Heuer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> He was concerned about a possible timekeeping error and asked representatives from TAG Heuer and the three race stewards for the Brazilian Grand Prix,<sup id="cite_ref-:1_85-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> to attend a meeting at the FIA headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> on the morning of 11 April as part of compliance with <i>Article 179 (b) of the <a href="/wiki/International_Sporting_Code" title="International Sporting Code">International Sporting Code</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-:0_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Oral arguments and timing evidence were presented to a <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA) court in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>, which, on April 11, awarded victory to Fisichella.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCRuling_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCRuling-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> McLaren declined to file an appeal. This was Fisichella's first Formula One win and the last for the Ford engine and Jordan team. An unofficial ceremony was held during <a href="/wiki/2003_San_Marino_Grand_Prix" title="2003 San Marino Grand Prix">the next race weekend</a> at <a href="/wiki/Autodromo_Enzo_e_Dino_Ferrari" class="mw-redirect" title="Autodromo Enzo e Dino Ferrari">Imola</a>, where Räikkönen and <a href="/wiki/Ron_Dennis" title="Ron Dennis">Ron Dennis</a> handed over the winning driver's and constructor's trophies to Fisichella and <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Jordan" title="Eddie Jordan">Eddie Jordan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Race_classification">Race classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Race classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_Brazilian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The podium ceremony featured Räikkönen in first place, Fisichella in second and no-one in third, as Alonso was receiving medical attention at the time. The <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> later reversed first and second place due to a timekeeping error.<sup id="cite_ref-GPCOMRace_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPCOMRace-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-26"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-26">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Ferrari's nominated reserve driver <a href="/wiki/Luca_Badoer" title="Luca Badoer">Luca Badoer</a> was injured in two high-speed accidents.<sup id="cite_ref-BarrichelloGP_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BarrichelloGP-25">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
